### [174] [All you need is log](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27349)
*Akshay Balsubramani*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文完整刻画了多分布Rényi散度族：满足数据处理单调性和乘积可加性的W元分布泛函，其全体由四层参数空间上的多路重合散度C_α的正积分构成，并通过五条独立公理化路径收敛于同一族，证明了这是多分布情形的标准Rényi演算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多问题需要同时比较多个分布（如多群体公平性、多先验PAC-Bayes界、多假设检验），但Rényi散度仅适用于两分布情形，多分布情形下Rényi族的正确推广长期悬而未决。

Method: 通过公理化刻画（数据处理单调性+乘积可加性）定义泛函空间；识别出四层参数结构：单纯形内部、混合符号指数锥（类比Rényi阶>1）、无穷远处的热带边界（最大散度）、单纯形顶点处的成对KL散度边界；并通过五条独立路线（结构公理、Kolmogorov-Nagumo均值+Rényi熵公理化、经典熵刻画、多假设检验误差指数、多彩票赌博解释）验证同一族的涌现。

Result: 所有满足单调性和可加性的W元分布泛函均为C_α散度在四层参数空间上的正积分；每层参数都是必要的且不可互相替代；两分布情形退化为标准Rényi结果。

Conclusion: 建立了多分布Rényi散度的完整图景，提供了规范的理论框架，并通过多路径独立复现证明了其作为"规范多分布Rényi演算"的普适性。

Abstract: Comparing two probability distributions is a basic building block of statistics and machine learning, and the right family is well understood: the Rényi divergences of order $α\in[0,\infty]$ are the unique family monotone under data processing and additive on independent products. Many problems instead compare more than two distributions at once -- multi-population fairness, multi-prior PAC-Bayes bounds, multi-hypothesis testing -- and the right multi-distribution generalization of the Rényi family has been an open question.
  We characterize it. Every functional of $W$-tuples of distributions that is monotone under data processing and additive on independent products is a positive integral of multi-way coincidence divergences $C_α(π_1,\dots,π_W) := -\log\int π_1^{α_1}\cdotsπ_W^{α_W}$ (with $\sum_k α_k = 1$) over a parameter space with four strata: the simplex interior; mixed-sign exponent cones (the analogue of Rényi orders $>1$); a tropical boundary at infinity carrying max-divergences; and pairwise Kullback-Leibler edges at the simplex vertices. Each stratum is necessary -- the destination of an explicit data-processing-monotone, product-additive divergence the others cannot reproduce -- and each is a clean limit of simplex-interior atoms.
  The same family arises from five independent routes -- the structural axioms, Kolmogorov-Nagumo means with Rényi's entropy axiomatics, classical entropy characterizations, multi-hypothesis testing error exponents, and a multi-lottery betting interpretation -- structural evidence that this is the canonical multi-distribution Rényi calculus rather than an artefact of any one axiomatic input. The two-prior case recovers the standard Rényi result; a worked $W=3$ instance, numerical verification, and a conditional extension round out the treatment.

</details>


<div id='cs.GR'></div>

### [175] [HiPR: Hierarchical Progressive Rendering for Immediate Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26612)
*Rafael Padilla,Andrew Tate,Dhruv Ram,Cem Yuksel*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: HiPR是一种动态渲染调度算法，通过基于优先级顺序分层更新像素，实现交互式路径追踪的实时光追体验，最终收敛到无偏结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统渲染器在场景变化后需要重新计算整个帧，导致交互响应延迟，无法实现实时感。本文旨在解决这一瓶颈，使得交互式路径追踪能够提供即时视觉反馈。

Method: 将像素组织成从变化元素向外传播的光路依赖层次结构，基于感知影响设定优先级，优先更新高优先级像素，保持其他像素不变，从而分层渐进式渲染。

Result: 实现了即时视觉反馈，最终收敛到无偏结果，相比传统全帧重计算方法大幅提升了交互响应速度。

Conclusion: HiPR通过分层优先级调度策略，在不牺牲最终渲染质量的前提下，显著提升了交互式路径追踪的实时感，是一种有效的动态渲染调度方案。

Abstract: Hierarchical Progressive Rendering (HiPR) is a dynamic render-scheduling algorithm that makes interactive path tracing finally feel real-time. While most renderers recompute the entire frame after any change to the scene, our method updates some of the pixels based on a priority order while keeping the others unchanged. Rather than relying on error-driven or temporal reuse heuristics, it amortizes rendering costs by organizing pixels into a hierarchy of light-path dependencies from changed elements outward, prioritizing by perceptual impact and delivering instant visual feedback, while eventually converging to an unbiased result.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在单色渲染下显著改善了外观保持性，同时在一致的热力学仿真设置下降低了应力集中；物理3D打印实例表明优化后的几何保留了更多可识别的视觉细节，同时保持可制造性。

Abstract: Recent advances in 3D mesh generation have enabled the creation of visually realistic assets. However, much of their visual fidelity is encoded in textures rather than geometry. When such assets are fabricated using monochromatic materials, texture information is largely lost, causing visually important details to disappear even when the original geometry is faithfully preserved. A key challenge is that the geometric perturbations required to recover texture-dependent appearance cues often introduce sharp local features and high-frequency surface structures, which may increase stress concentration and fabrication risk. In this paper, we present GenMF, an appearance-oriented geometry refinement framework for monochromatic fabrication. GenMF transforms texture-dependent visual cues into geometry-induced shading effects and formulates geometry refinement as a balance between appearance preservation and fabrication-oriented robustness. To discourage structurally and narrow the gap between simulation and physical manufacturing, we further introduce a differentiable stress-aware regularization based on a learned thermal-stress predictor. Experimental results demonstrate that GenMF significantly improves appearance preservation under monochromatic rendering while reducing stress concentration under a consistent thermo-mechanical simulation setting. Physical 3D printing examples further show that the refined geometries preserve more recognizable visual details while remaining suitable for fabrication. These results suggest that appearance-aware geometry refinement provides an effective bridge between generated 3D assets and fabrication-ready monochromatic objects.

### [179] [Multiscale Exit-Join Dynamics: Tactical Consensus and Strategic Coalition Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26139)
*Quanyan Zhu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个多尺度联盟形成模型，将战略性退出与加入决策与联盟内部的战术共识动态相耦合。联盟价值内生于联盟内的信息聚合过程，同时采用Aumann-Dreze支付、转换摩擦和接受规则来约束战略性重组。该框架引入快-慢架构：可转移的联盟价值从DeGroot式共识过程中涌现，而联盟结构则通过激励驱动的退出与加入动态演化。分析刻画了联合战术-战略均衡、战术与战略一致性的条件、隔离、极化以及维持稳定联盟结构的认知障碍。建立了耦合动态的不动点刻画与存在性结果。数值实验揭示了一个"不稳定-共识悖论"：低或负的转换障碍可能阻碍战略收敛，同时却能促进足够的时间混合以实现全局战术共识。结果为多智能体系统中的联盟形成、共识动态、信息聚合与战略稳定性提供了统一视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常将联盟形成与内部共识过程分离处理，未能捕捉二者之间的双向耦合关系。本文旨在构建一个统一框架，同时刻画战略层面的联盟重组决策与战术层面的内部意见动态，以理解联盟价值如何内生于信息聚合、以及转换摩擦如何影响系统稳定性和共识达成。

Method: 采用多尺度建模方法，将快尺度上的DeGroot式共识过程（生成可转移联盟价值）与慢尺度上基于Aumann-Dreze支付的激励驱动退出与加入决策相耦合。通过不动点理论刻画联合均衡，辅以数值实验验证理论预测。

Result: 建立了联合战术-战略均衡的存在性定理；刻画了战术与战略一致性的充分条件；揭示了隔离、极化及认知障碍对稳定性的影响；发现"不稳定-共识悖论"：低或负转换障碍反而能通过时间混合促进全局共识。

Conclusion: 该框架为理解多智能体系统中联盟形成的战略与战术层面提供了统一视角，突出展示了转换摩擦的非单调效应以及信息聚合对联盟结构的反馈机制。

Abstract: This paper develops a multiscale model of coalition formation in which strategic exit-and-join decisions are coupled with tactical consensus dynamics inside coalitions. Coalition value is generated endogenously from within-coalition information aggregation, while Aumann-Dreze payoffs, switching frictions, and acceptance rules govern strategic reconfiguration. The framework introduces a fast-slow architecture in which transferable coalition value emerges from DeGroot-style consensus processes, while coalition structures evolve through incentive-driven exit-and-join dynamics. The analysis characterizes joint tactical-strategic equilibria, conditions for tactical and strategic unanimity, segregation, polarization, and cognitive barriers that sustain stable coalition structures. A fixed-point characterization and existence results are established for the coupled dynamics. Numerical experiments reveal an instability-consensus paradox: low or negative switching barriers may prevent strategic convergence while simultaneously promoting temporal mixing sufficient to achieve global tactical consensus. The results provide a unified perspective on coalition formation, consensus dynamics, information aggregation, and strategic stability in multi-agent systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作[GSW STOC'25]提出了基于单样本的在线资源分配学习算法，但存在两个问题：一是动态定价算法导致不同代理面临不同价格，引发公平性问题；二是该算法需要预先知道代理的到达顺序。为解决这些问题，本文研究匿名定价算法的学习性。

Method: 利用样本和定价查询来学习匿名定价算法。具体通过两个结果：1) 证明多项式数量的样本足以学习经典对偶定价算法；2) 证明多项式数量的定价查询足以学习近优匿名定价算法，其中每个代理面临的物品定价向量来自同一个预定分布。

Result: 1) 多项式数量的样本可学习经典对偶定价算法；2) 多项式数量的定价查询可学习近优匿名定价算法。

Abstract: We study the online resource allocation problem, where a seller sequentially receives independent requests for $m$ types of resources with limited supplies from $n$ heterogeneous agents arriving in an unknown order. Each request from an agent can be fulfilled in different ways, with resource consumption in $[0,1]^m$, and generates different values for the agent. The objective of the seller is to maximize the social welfare, which is the sum of the values obtained from each agent.
  Recently, Ghuge, Singla, and Wang [GSW STOC'25] studied the learnability of the online resource allocation problem with heterogeneous agents and proposed a learnable pricing algorithm using only a single sample. However, their core algorithm is a dynamic pricing algorithm, which may introduce fairness concerns, as different agents face different prices. Furthermore, the algorithm crucially needs to know the arrival order of the agents in advance. To address these issues, in this paper, we study the learnability of anonymous pricing algorithms for online resource allocation using samples and queries to agents' value distributions. First, we show that a polynomial number of samples suffices to learn the classic dual pricing algorithm. Second, we show that a polynomial number of pricing queries suffices to learn a near-optimal anonymous pricing algorithm, in which the item pricing vector faced by each agent is drawn from the same predetermined distribution.

### [182] [Almost EFX in Hypergraphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26948)
*Ioannis Kakatelis,Thanasis Lianeas,Alkmini Sgouritsa,Minas Marios Sotiriou*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究超图（多重边）设置下不可分物品的EFX分配问题。在周长为至少3的超图中，针对一般单调估值提出了EF2X分配的更简单构造；在边重数为2时，对加性估值证明了EF3X分配的存在性。在近似EFX方面，针对次加性估值给出了√2/2-EFX分配的更简单构造，并将边重数为2时加性估值下的最优近似界推进至2/3-EFX。所有构造均为多项式或伪多项式时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用构造性方法：（1）利用超图的周长为至少3的结构特性，简化EF2X分配的构造；（2）对于边重数为2的加性估值，通过更精细的分配策略实现EF3X；（3）在近似EFX方面，分别针对次加性估值设计√2/2-EFX的简单构造，以及针对重数为2的加性估值给出2/3-EFX的构造。

Result: 在超图（周长为至少3）和多重边设置下，给出了EF2X、EF3X分配的存在性证明及多项式时间构造；将近似EFX的比率从已有的结果提升至√2/2（次加性估值）和2/3（重数为2的加性估值），后者为伪多项式时间构造。

Conclusion: 本文通过简化和推广已有构造，在超图与多重边设置下推进了EFX及相关公平分配问题的理论进展，为未来解决一般设置下的EFX存在性问题提供了新的思路和工具。

Abstract: We study the existence of envy-free-up-to-any-good (EFX) allocations of indivisible goods among agents with heterogeneous monotone valuations. Christodoulou et al. (2023) introduced the (multi-hyper)graph setting, where agents and goods are represented by vertices and edges of a graph respectively, and only the endpoints of an edge may have non-zero marginal value for it. Our work simplifies and extends previous results of Kaviani et al. (Alireza Kaviani, Masoud Seddighin, Amir Mohammad Shahrezaei. Almost Envy-Free Allocation of Indivisible Goods: A Tale of Two Valuations. WINE 2024) in this domain. First, we provide a simpler construction of EF2X allocation for general monotone valuations in hypergraphs with girth at least 3. We extend our ideas when the multiplicity of each edge is 2 and show that an EF3X allocation always exists for additive valuations. Both results can be constructed in polynomial time. Regarding EFX approximations, we provide a simpler construction for $\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$-EFX allocations in hypergraphs of girth at least 3 under subadditive valuations. We push the state-of-the-art by establishing the existence of $\frac{2}{3}$-EFX allocations for additive valuations when the edge multiplicity is 2. Both of the latter results can be constructed in pseudo-polynomial time. By addressing these multi-hypergraph settings, our work contributes to the ongoing effort to resolve the existence of EFX in increasingly general and applicable domains.

### [183] [Parametric Open Source Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27068)
*Aleksandar Todorov,Jesse ten Napel,Alexander Müller*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开源博弈研究多基于离散或符号程序，缺乏连续可微的数学框架，难以分析梯度下降等连续优化行为对合作涌现的影响。

Method: 引入参数化开源博弈，玩家选择连续参数向量，通过语义映射将完整参数剖面转化为底层有限博弈的混合策略；建立均衡存在性定理，推导对称2×2博弈中自私梯度上升从背叛转向合作的精确耦合阈值，给出参数化程序纳什均衡的一维边界检验；扩展至神经语义类，导出由交叉玩家与自身玩家灵敏度比率控制的一阶合作条件。

Result: 在对称2×2博弈中获得了叛变-合作的精确耦合阈值；给出了参数化程序纳什均衡的一维边界检验；神经语义类中，一阶合作条件由交叉/自身灵敏度比率决定；经典博弈中展示了内部参数化访问如何定性重塑学习动力学和均衡结构。

Conclusion: 足够强的开源耦合能够引导自私优化走向合作结果，框架揭示了访问对手内部参数化可改变博弈均衡的定性特征。

Abstract: Open-source game theory studies agents whose behavior may depend on one another's decision procedures, but most existing models use discrete or symbolic programs. We introduce parametric open-source games, a continuous analogue of program equilibria in which players choose parameter vectors and semantics maps convert the full parameter profile into mixed actions in an underlying finite game. We establish equilibrium existence results, derive an exact coupling threshold at which selfish gradient ascent in symmetric $2\times2$ games switches from defection toward cooperation, and give a one-dimensional boundary test for parametric program Nash equilibria. We further extend the framework to a neural semantics class whose first-order cooperation condition is governed by the ratio of cross-player to self-player sensitivity. Across canonical games, the framework shows how access to internal parameterizations can qualitatively reshape learning dynamics and equilibrium structure, and how sufficiently strong open-source coupling can steer selfish optimization toward cooperative outcomes.

</details>

### [184] [Preference Optimization Drives Monoculture in LLM Prediction Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26583)
*James Begin,Brendan Gho,Suman Muppavarapu,Tyson Tsay,Atharva Mohan,Afnan Shaik,Ruizhe Li,Vasu Sharma,Archana Vaidheeswaran*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: LLM智能体在预测市场中存在高误差相关性（ρ=0.70），导致10个智能体的有效预测能力仅相当于约1.4个独立预测者，且增加智能体数量无法缓解，偏好优化是因果驱动因素，跨模型多样性是最有效的缓解方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究当预测市场中的交易者由LLM智能体构成时，参与者误差独立性假设是否仍然成立。

Method: 通过DPO微调LLM智能体，测量成对误差相关性（ρ）和有效预测者数量（N_eff），进行受控消融实验隔离偏好优化的因果效应，并测试多种缓解策略。

Result: LLM智能体间误差相关性高达ρ=0.70，10个智能体的N_eff仅约1.4；增加智能体数量（N=5到40）无法提升N_eff；10智能体市场（67.6%）表现不如单个独立智能体（70.2%）；偏好优化导致相关性增加Δρ=+0.24至+0.46；跨模型多样性将ρ从0.68降至0.40。

Conclusion: LLM越对齐，基于它们构建的预测市场越趋于单一文化，误差独立性被破坏，市场预测能力受限。

Abstract: Prediction markets rest on the independence of participant errors. As LLM agents become active traders on platforms like Kalshi and Polymarket, we ask: does this independence hold when the crowd is composed of LLMs? We find it does not. LLM agents fine-tuned with Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) share a convergent output distribution, producing pairwise error correlations of $ρ= 0.70$ and reducing ten agents to the effective forecasting power of ${\approx}1.4$ independent forecasters $N_{\text{eff}}$. This is not a scaling problem: $N_{\text{eff}}$ remains flat from $N=5$ to $N=40$, and the 10-agent market (67.6%) fails to match a single standalone agent (70.2%). Two controlled ablations isolate preference optimization as the causal driver, replicated across labs and scales ($Δρ= +0.24$ to $+0.46$ on identical-SFT controls at 8B and 70B). Among mitigations tested, cross-model diversity achieves the largest correlation reduction ($ρ$ from 0.68 to 0.40). As LLMs become more aligned, markets built from them become more monocultural.

</details>


### [185] [Holistic Multivariance Decomposition: Adapting Mode Interrelations in Low-Rank Tensor Approximations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26965)
*Süha Tuna*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出Holistic Multivariance Decomposition (HMD)框架，通过显式建模张量中模式的独立效应与高阶交互关系，克服了传统Tucker和CP分解忽略模式间相互耦合的结构性局限。在三个跨领域基准测试中，HMD相比传统方法持续取得更低的重建误差，成为高保真处理复杂多维耦合数据的鲁棒方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Tucker和CP分解将张量表示为模式间外积求和的形式，本质仅捕捉各模式的独立变化，系统性地忽略了张量中天然嵌入的模式间相互作用与维度耦合依赖关系。这种结构性局限促使作者提出一个能同时建模孤立模式效应与高阶相互关系的张量分解框架。

Method: 提出HMD框架，通过设计专门的投影算子显式建模两类信息：1) 孤立模式效应（各模式的独立贡献）；2) 高阶相互关系（模式间的耦合作用）。该算法在传统张量分解基础上引入更丰富的结构表达能力。

Result: 在三个来自不同领域的基准测试上，HMD框架在重建误差指标上持续显著低于Tucker分解和CP分解，验证了其高保真度。

Conclusion: HMD作为一种鲁棒、高保真的计算方法，能够有效解析科学与工程应用中复杂、深度耦合的多维数据结构，弥补了经典张量分解方法在捕捉模式间相互依赖方面的结构性缺陷。

Abstract: Low-rank tensor approximation is a foundational tool for multidimensional data analysis in scientific computing, classically dominated by Tucker and Canonical Polyadic (CP) decompositions. While widely adopted, these standard approximation schemes represent data as sums of rank-1 tensors formed via mode-wise outer products. This inherent mathematical structure captures the independent variations of individual modes but systematically neglects the mutual interactions and coupled dimensional interdependencies natively embedded within the tensor. To overcome this structural limitation, we introduce the Holistic Multivariance Decomposition (HMD) framework. HMD provides a novel tensor decomposition algorithm that explicitly models both isolated mode effects and higher order mutual relationships through specialized projection operators. Numerical evaluations focusing on three distinct benchmarks from various fields demonstrate that the proposed HMD framework consistently yields significantly lower reconstruction errors compared to both Tucker and CP decomposition. These results establish HMD as a robust, high fidelity computational method for resolving complex, deeply coupled multidimensional data structures in science and engineering applications.

</details>


### [186] [Latent Diffusion Posterior Sampling with Surrogate Likelihood Guidance for PDE Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26592)
*Yuanzhe Wang,Alexandre M. Tartakovsky*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出了一种潜在空间扩散后验采样（L-DPS）框架，用于高维PDE约束逆问题，通过VAE降维、潜在扩散模型学习隐式先验、扩散后验采样结合似然引导，并利用神经网络代理避免重复调用全阶PDE求解器。在逆达西流问题中表现出准确、鲁棒的逆解，降低了推理成本，优于多种基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PDE约束逆问题面临三大挑战：基于样本的隐式先验缺乏可处理密度、高维空间分布参数、后验采样中反复调用正演模型计算成本高昂。现有方法如全空间扩散后验采样计算负担重，而变分推断等摊销方法在稀疏噪声场景下性能有限。

Method: L-DPS结合四个组件：VAE将参数场映射到低维潜在空间；无条件潜在扩散模型在潜在空间学习隐式先验得分；扩散后验采样（DPS）将学习到的先验与似然引导相结合；可微神经代理（解码器-代理组合）计算似然梯度，避免重复调用全阶数值PDE求解器。

Result: 在逆达西流问题（从稀疏含噪压力观测推断未知空间分布渗透率场）中，L-DPS产生准确鲁棒的逆解；相比全空间DPS降低了推理成本；在稀疏和噪声场景下优于条件潜在扩散和逆FNO等摊销逆基线；进一步与KLE-MAP基线进行了比较，并研究了混合先验泛化能力及代理正演模型误差对反演精度的影响。

Conclusion: L-DPS为高维PDE约束逆问题提供了一种近似贝叶斯框架，有效平衡了计算效率与反演精度，特别适用于先验仅为样本形式、参数高维且正演模型昂贵的问题场景。

Abstract: We propose latent-space diffusion posterior sampling (L-DPS), an approximate Bayesian framework for high-dimensional inverse problems governed by partial differential equations (PDEs). The method addresses three challenges in PDE-constrained inversion: implicit sample-based priors without tractable densities, high-dimensional spatially distributed parameters, and the high cost of repeated forward-model evaluations during posterior sampling. L-DPS combines a variational autoencoder, an unconditional latent diffusion model, diffusion posterior sampling, and a differentiable neural surrogate. The VAE maps the parameter field to a lower-dimensional latent space, the diffusion model learns an implicit prior score in this latent space, and DPS combines this learned prior with likelihood-based guidance. The likelihood gradient is evaluated through the decoder-surrogate composition, avoiding repeated calls to the full numerical PDE solver. We evaluate the method on an inverse Darcy flow problem with an unknown spatially distributed permeability field inferred from sparse and noisy pressure observations. L-DPS produces accurate and robust inverse solutions, reduces inference cost relative to full-space DPS, and outperforms amortized inverse baselines such as conditional latent diffusion and inverse FNO in sparse and noisy regimes. We further compare L-DPS with a KLE-MAP baseline and study mixed-prior generalization and the sensitivity of inversion accuracy to surrogate forward-model error.

### [187] [A hybrid IFENN solver for generalizable modeling of phase-field fracture initiation and propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27177)
*Panos Pantidis,Fouad Amin,Diab Abueidda,Mostafa E. Mobasher*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出IFENN框架，通过DeepOKAN（初始阶段）和CNN（扩展阶段）混合建模相场断裂全过程，仅用少量训练增量和高斯点即可实现跨几何泛化，并引入人工边界条件改善远场预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统相场断裂模拟计算成本高昂，IFENN将FEM与预训练NN混合可提升效率，但现有方法在跨几何泛化和训练效率上仍有不足，亟需一种能高效建模断裂全过程且可泛化的混合方案。

Method: 采用IFENN混合框架，FEM求解力学平衡，两个网络分别近似相场扩散方程：DeepOKAN处理初始阶段，CNN处理扩展阶段。网络仅基于基准几何以物理信息方式训练，使用极少训练增量和从断裂过程区策略采样的有限高斯点，并引入人工边界条件改进预测外推。

Result: 在训练和未见几何上均展示了方法的灵活性和数值精度，显著降低了离线训练成本。

Conclusion: IFENN结合DeepOKAN与CNN可高效、准确地建模相场断裂全过程，具有良好的跨几何泛化能力，且训练成本极低。

Abstract: In this paper we demonstrate how the Integrated Finite Element Neural Network (IFENN) framework can effectively model the entire evolution of phase-field fracture, including the initiation and propagation stage, across generalizable geometries. IFENN is a hybrid scheme for coupled computational mechanics problems, tightly coupling a standard FEM solver (mechanical equilibrium) with a pre-trained neural network (coupled field). In this work, the phase-field diffusion equation is approximated with: i) a DeepONet architecture with Kolmogorov-Arnold networks in the trunk and branch (DeepOKAN) for the initiation stage, and ii) a Convolution Neural Network (CNN) for the propagation stage. Both networks are trained only once, on a benchmark geometry, using a purely physics-informed approach based on the maximum strain energy and the phase-field variable. The training process utilizes an extremely small number of training increments and only a limited number of Gauss points that are strategically sampled from the fracture process zone. These features enable a substantial decrease of the offline training cost. To address the extrapolation of the DeepOKAN predictions in regions away from the crack tip during the inference stage, we implement a set of artificial boundary conditions to enforce the near-zero values in the far-field predictions. We showcase the flexibility and numerical accuracy of the proposed methodology across both the training and unseen geometries.

### [188] [Detecting and Controlling Sycophancy with Cascading Linear Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26155)

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于激活引导的方法需要大量高质量的对比样本对来可靠地检测和引导模型行为，但传统二元对比样本难以充分解耦复杂行为背后的特征。

Method: 提出迭代数据生成管道，构建展现行为线性变化的级联样本，而非简单的二元对比样本，从而更好地解耦线性特征。以语言模型的谄媚行为为例进行验证。

Result: 级联样本发现的谄媚特征形成线性可分子空间；在检测、确定性评分和稳健引导任务上匹配或超越LLM-as-a-judge和系统提示基线方法，同时计算需求更低、可解释性更强。

Abstract: Interpreting and controlling model behaviors through activation steering methods requires many pairs of contrastive samples that clearly exhibit desired or undesired behavior. These data pairs determine the degree to which interpretability frameworks can reliably detect model features responsible for a behavior, and therefore the ability to steer models toward or away from such behavior. In this work, we present an iterative data generation pipeline that isolates cascading linear features responsible for a behavior. Specifically, we show how moving beyond simple binary pairs of samples, and instead isolating samples that show degrees of features that scale linearly with behavior, allows for better disentanglement of features. We focus on detecting and steering away from sycophancy -- the tendency of language models to prioritize user validation. We demonstrate that sycophancy features discovered through cascading samples form linearly separable subspaces, and allow for selection of model activations that more clearly correspond to the desired behavior than baseline approaches. We also evaluate their ability to enable detection, deterministic scoring, and robust steering, and see that they either match or outperform LLM-as-a-judge and system prompting baselines while providing lower computational demand and more interpretability guarantees. Code & Data: https://cascading-feats.github.io/

### [189] [Life After Benchmark Saturation: A Case Study of CORE-Bench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26158)
*Nitya Nadgir,Sayash Kapoor,Kangheng Liu,Peter Kirgis,Matilda Orona,Stephan Rabanser,Tilman Bayer,Abhishek Shetty,Yue Ling,Derrick Chan-Sew,Rumi Nakagawa,Saiteja Utpala,Zachary S. Siegel,Arvind Narayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文挑战了当前以准确率为核心的基准评测范式，提出在准确率饱和后仍可从构造效度、泛化性、效率、可靠性、模型与脚手架相对重要性、人机协作增益等六个维度评估智能体性能。以CORE-Bench Hard（科学代码可复现性基准）为案例，揭示了构造效度威胁，发布了改进版基准CORE-Bench v1.1和OOD套件，并通过小规模随机实验发现人机协作可带来约两倍的统计显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基准评测在准确率饱和后往往被直接废弃，忽视了从其他关键维度继续评估智能体性能的机会，需要一种更全面的评测范式。

Method: 以CORE-Bench Hard为案例，识别构造效度威胁并发布改进版本CORE-Bench v1.1和OOD套件；在准确率饱和后测量效率、可靠性、模型/脚手架性能；进行小规模随机实验测量人机协作增益。

Result: 发现了难以被早期弱智能体预见的构造效度问题；CORE-Bench v1.1在准确率饱和后仍可用于测量多个维度；人机协作带来约两倍的统计显著加速，且该结果可能被低估（因五分之一的纯人工复现任务超时未完成）。

Conclusion: 提出了一种比传统准确率中心评测范式更严格的替代方案，强调在准确率饱和后仍可对智能体进行多维度的有意义评估。

Abstract: When a benchmark's accuracy saturates, it is often retired and replaced with a more challenging version. We show that this approach privileges accuracy and misses the opportunity to study six other key dimensions of agent performance: construct validity issues such as shortcuts, out-of-distribution generalizability, efficiency, reliability, the relative importance of the model versus the scaffold, and uplift from human-agent collaboration. We use CORE-Bench Hard, a benchmark for computational reproducibility of scientific code, as a case study to demonstrate that measuring agents along these dimensions yields meaningful insights into agent performance even after accuracy saturates. First, we surface threats to construct validity in CORE-Bench Hard that are difficult to anticipate with less capable agents. We introduce an improved benchmark, CORE-Bench v1.1, and an out-of-distribution task suite, CORE-Bench OOD. Second, we find that despite accuracy saturation, CORE-Bench v1.1 remains useful for measuring efficiency, reliability, model performance, and scaffold performance. Finally, we conduct a small-scale randomized experiment to measure uplift from human-agent collaboration on real-world computational reproducibility tasks. We find a statistically significant speedup by about a factor of two -- likely underestimated due to one-fifth of human-only reproductions reaching the time limit before completing -- and describe various other findings. Together, our contributions present a more rigorous alternative to the dominant accuracy-centric evaluation paradigm.

### [190] [Refusal Lives Downstream of Persona in Chat Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26161)
*Viola Zhong,Qirui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现指令微调模型中的服从人格方向会门控拒绝方向：增强服从人格会抑制拒绝行为（如Llama中拒绝率从97%降至2%），拒绝仅在后期层通过人格门控实现表达，而非独立机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究分别识别了激活空间中的拒绝方向和人格特质方向，但两者被视为独立机制。本文旨在探究它们之间的相互作用关系。

Method: 在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct中提取服从模型人格方向和拒绝方向，通过干预（增强/投射去除）两者来观察行为变化。

Result: 服从人格方向抑制拒绝（Llama中拒绝率从97%降至2%）；后期层重新引入拒绝方向可部分恢复拒绝；在后期层窗口投射去除人格方向可恢复基准拒绝率，随机方向则不能。

Conclusion: 拒绝在后期表达阶段受人格门控，位于其计算阶段的下游；将拒绝视为孤立的独立方向会忽略其对人格的依赖性。

Abstract: Linear directions in activation space have been identified for both refusal and persona traits in instruction-tuned chat models, but the two have been studied as separate mechanisms. We show they interact: a compliant persona gates refusal. In Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we extract a compliant model-persona direction and a refusal direction and intervene on both. Compliant persona steering suppresses refusal -- in Llama, the refusal rate falls from 97% to 2%. Reintroducing the refusal direction partially restores refusal at late layers but not at early ones. Projecting out the persona direction in a late-layer window restores it to baseline; projecting out a random direction does not. Refusal is therefore gated at the late-layer expression stage, downstream of where it is computed. Treating refusal as a single isolated direction misses its dependence on persona.

</details>


### [191] [AlgoEvolve: LLM-driven Meta-evolution of Algorithmic Trading Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26173)
*Dhruv Sharma,Gautam Shroff*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AlgoEvolve，一个基于LLM驱动的进化框架，用于在算法交易领域自动生成、评估和迭代改进可执行的交易策略。系统展现出涌现性的自适应策略逻辑，并引入元进化外层循环自动优化提示词搜索启发式，在复杂环境中持续进行程序合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究展示了LLM可以作为语义变异算子用于程序和证明的进化发现，但大多数应用局限于静态编码基准测试。算法交易领域因其噪声性、非平稳性和高度不连续性而具有独特挑战，作者希望将LLM驱动的进化范式拓展到这一复杂领域。

Method: 提出AlgoEvolve框架：内层循环使用LLM作为语义变异算子生成Python代码形式的交易策略，并通过严格的测试协议进行评估和迭代改进；外层循环是元进化过程，自动演化用于指导内层程序合成的提示词，以发现更优的搜索启发式。

Result: 系统展现出涌现性的自适应策略逻辑，能够自主切换交易规则；元进化外层循环发现了改进的搜索启发式，在平衡探索与利用的同时减少了零交易失败，且持续优于初始人工设计的指令。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的语义进化为复杂环境中的持续程序合成提供了一种可行方法，在算法交易这一噪声性、非平稳性、高不连续性的领域展现出良好效果。

Abstract: Recent work shows that Large Language Models (LLMs) can act as semantic mutation operators for the evolutionary discovery of programs and proofs. Most current applications focus on static coding benchmarks. We extend this paradigm to algorithmic trading. This domain is uniquely challenging because it is noisy, non-stationary, and highly discontinuous. We present AlgoEvolve, an LLM-driven evolutionary framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively improves executable trading strategies. These strategies are expressed as Python code and evaluated through a rigorous testing protocol. Across multiple experiments, the system exhibits emergent regime-adaptive strategy logic, including autonomous shifts in trading rules. We further introduce a meta-evolutionary outer loop that evolves the prompts guiding program synthesis in the inner loop. This outer loop discovers improved search heuristics. These heuristics balance exploration and exploitation while reducing zero-trade failures. They consistently outperform initial human-designed instructions. The results demonstrate that LLM-based semantic evolution provides a viable approach for continual program synthesis in complex environments.

Abstract: As AI agent protocols proliferate, the governance structures shaping their interoperability standards remain empirically underexamined. Discourse alignment is denser in the permissionless setting, suggesting that open governance may foster greater thematic convergence despite decentralized participation. ### [193] [Knowledge-augmented Agentic AI for Mental Health Medication Information Seeking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26205)
*Huizi Yu,Jian Liu,Wenkong Wang,Lingyao Li,Jiayan Zhou,Zhaoqian Xue,Xiang Li,Xinxin Lin,Zhiying Liang,Zhuoru Wu,Siyuan Ma,Xin Ma,Lizhou Fan*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于知识图谱的多智能体框架，将466,525条Reddit帖子、60,782条WebMD评论和二十年FDA不良事件报告系统数据整合在一起，用于九种抗抑郁药物的安全信息分析。研究发现患者生成的数据与监管报告形成独立的安全信号，且许多不良事件在社区来源中比FDA报告早出现数百天。该框架通过ATC-N、ICD-10和MedDRA词汇体系保持数据来源可追溯，区分监管事实与患者经验。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 两个社区平台（Reddit和WebMD）之间的Jaccard相似度高达0.905，远高于它们与FDA报告的一致性，表明患者生成数据构成部分独立的安全信号。对于舍曲林，许多不良事件在社区来源中出现的时间比FDA报告中对应的日期早数百天。

Abstract: Patients increasingly seek medication information online, yet safety knowledge for psychiatric drugs is split between regulatory adverse-event records, which are authoritative but abstract, and patient narratives, which are experience-near but unvalidated. Here we develop a provenance-aware, knowledge-graph-based multi-agent framework unifying 466,525 Reddit posts, 60,782 WebMD reviews, and twenty years of U.S. FDA Adverse Event Reporting System records for nine antidepressants. A large-language-model entity-recognition pipeline benchmarked against physician annotations reached highest F1 scores of 0.969 for medications and 0.973 for conditions. For sertraline, many adverse events appeared in community sources hundreds of days before the corresponding FDA date. A Neo4j knowledge graph grounded in ATC-N, ICD-10, and MedDRA vocabularies preserves provenance, keeping every claim traceable and regulatory facts distinct from patient experience. These results establish source-aware integration as a route to more auditable psychiatric medication information, with usefulness and patient benefit to be tested prospectively.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 借鉴人类机构治理强大自主行动者的制度模式，形式化为计算治理模型：代理保留全部自主权但无执行权；高风险行动的执行依赖于预先声明的条件，每个条件由独立权威来源加密认证，并由确定性策略评估；决策记录在防篡改日志中。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents may begin to perform consequential, irreversible actions such as clinical prescribing and production software deployment. This paper observes that human institutions have governed powerful autonomous actors not by monitoring their reasoning but by requiring independently attested evidence at the point of consequential action. We formalise this institutional pattern as a computational governance model for AI agent systems. Under the proposed model, an agent retains full autonomy over planning and reasoning but holds no execution authority over designated high-risk actions. Execution is conditional on preconditions that are each independently attested by a separate authoritative source, cryptographically bound to a declared intent, and evaluated by a deterministic policy. Decisions are recorded in a tamper-evident log amenable to independent re-verification. We present a proof-of-concept implementation and illustrate the model with examples from software deployment and clinical prescribing.

### [197] [The Verification Horizon: No Silver Bullet for Coding Agent Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26300)
*Binghai Wang,Chenlong Zhang,Dayiheng Liu,Jiajun Zhang,Jiawei Chen,Mouxiang Chen,Rongyao Fang,Siyuan Zhang,Xuwu Wang,Yuheng Jing,Zeyao Ma,Zeyu Cui*

TL;DR: 随着编码智能体能力增强，验证比生成更难；验证信号需同时具备可扩展性、忠实性和鲁棒性；奖励函数需随策略能力共同进化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典直觉认为验证比生成容易，但当前编码智能体中这一关系被颠倒：生成复杂候选解已不困难，可靠验证反而成为更难的问题。现有验证器仅是人类意图的代理，存在先天不足。

Method: 从可扩展性、忠实性和鲁棒性三个维度刻画验证信号质量；研究四种奖励构造：测试验证器（通用编码）、规则验证器（前端任务）、用户作为验证器（真实世界智能体任务）、自动智能体验证器（长时域任务），并在不同任务类型和策略能力层级下进行实验分析。

Result: 针对性验证设计能有效抑制奖励黑客行为，提升任务完成质量，在多个内部和公开基准上取得显著提升。

Conclusion: 不存在固定奖励函数能在策略能力持续增长时保持有效；验证必须与生成器共同进化。

Abstract: A classical intuition holds that verifying a solution is easier than producing one. For today's coding agents, this intuition is being inverted: as foundation models develop stronger reasoning capabilities and engineering harnesses grow more sophisticated, generating complex candidate solutions is no longer difficult -- reliably verifying them has become the harder problem. Every verifier we can build is only a proxy for human intent, never the intent itself. This makes verification subject to a twofold difficulty: first, intent is underspecified by nature, making it inherently hard to faithfully check whether it has been fulfilled; second, during model training, optimization widens the gap between proxy and intent -- manifesting as reward hacking or signal saturation. To address this, we characterize the quality of verification signals along three dimensions -- scalability, faithfulness, and robustness -- and argue that achieving all three simultaneously is the central challenge. We further study four reward constructions: a test verifier for general coding tasks, a rubric verifier for frontend tasks, the user as verifier for real-world agent tasks, and an automated agent verifier for long-horizon tasks. Across different task types and policy capability levels, we conduct in-depth analysis and experiments on the core challenges of reward design and how to more effectively leverage reward signals. Experiments show that targeted verification design can effectively suppress reward hacking, improve task completion quality, and achieve significant gains across multiple internal and public benchmarks. These experiences collectively point to a core observation: no fixed reward function can remain effective as policy capability continues to grow; and verification must co-evolve with the generator.

Motivation: 现有量化金融智能体评估碎片化，各平台通常只关注单一任务，无法反映多阶段工作流的真实表现，容易高估智能体能力，难以揭示其在泛化、真实市场交互和金融意义决策上的弱点。

Method: 构建统一的gym环境，包含自动化任务构建流水线（将量化金融论文转为可执行任务包）、容器化运行时与主机端验证服务、低延迟纸面交易引擎、延迟解析机制（支持长周期和事件市场预测）、以及SFT和RL后训练集成。

Result: 提供了覆盖预测、市场生成、实时交易、欺诈检测的统一执行与验证接口，支持可扩展的智能体部署，防止运行时的训练-测试泄漏。

Conclusion: OpenFinGym通过统一多阶段任务和自动化构建机制，解决了量化金融智能体评估碎片化和金融相关性不足的问题，为智能体在真实市场环境下的能力评估和训练提供了全栈平台。

Abstract: Although large language model agents are increasingly applied to quantitative-finance workflows, their evaluation remains fragmented across isolated tasks, while the financial relevance of benchmark tasks is often overlooked. Yet financial workflows are inherently multi-stage, spanning interdependent tasks such as forecasting, strategy construction, risk management, and trading. Existing platforms typically focus on a single task, and can therefore overstate agent competence and fail to reveal weaknesses in generalization, real-market interaction, and financially meaningful decision-making. We introduce OpenFinGym, a unified gym environment for quantitative-finance agent development that covers forecasting, market generation, real-time trading, and fraud detection under a single execution and verification interface. OpenFinGym additionally provides an automated task-construction pipeline that turns quantitative finance publications into executable task packages; a containerised runtime with a host-side verifier service that supports scalable agent rollouts and prevents runtime train-test leakage; a paper trading engine with a low-latency data-stream design; deferred-resolution support for long-horizon and event-market forecasts; and integration for SFT and RL post-training

### [201] [Instruction Bleed: Cross-Module Interference in Prompt-Composed Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26356)
*Ching-Yu Lin,Yifan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出并形式化了提示组合式智能体系统中的组合行为泄漏（CBL）问题，即编辑一个提示模块会静默地改变其他模块的行为。通过部署的工作评估智能体实验，发现内容通道会产生可检测的配对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63），虽不翻转推荐结果，但在数千次决策中会累积影响。CBL与已知的智能体故障维度正交，需要作为提示组合式智能体评估的必要考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实践中发现，编辑提示组合式智能体系统中的一个提示模块会静默地改变其他模块的行为，尽管它们之间没有共享变量或可执行依赖关系。这种故障模式需要在理论上进行形式化和系统化研究。

Method: 通过可重复的三通道协议（volume、content、form）对部署的工作评估智能体（Claude Sonnet 4.6，144次试验）进行探测，扰动非焦点模块，并使用Cohen's d和bootstrap置信区间评估效应大小。

Result: 仅内容通道产生可检测的配对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63，bootstrap 95% CI排除零）；没有推荐结果被翻转，但效应处于次阈值状态，在智能体数千次决策中会累积。

Conclusion: CBL与已知的智能体故障维度（对抗性注入、认知退化、多智能体故障传播、隐私泄露）正交，需要将跨模块干扰测量纳入提示组合式智能体评估的必要要求。

Abstract: Practitioners of prompt-composed agentic systems report a recurring failure mode: editing one prompt module silently shifts the behavior of others despite no shared variable or executable dependency. We formalize this as compositional behavioral leakage (CBL): interference between modules sharing a context window. CBL is enabled by architectural non-isolation: transformer self-attention provides no formal boundary between concatenated modules. We probe CBL on a deployed job-evaluation agent (Claude Sonnet 4.6, 144 trials) through a reusable three-channel protocol that perturbs non-focal modules along volume, content, and form. Only the content channel produces a detectable paired effect (Cohen's d = 0.63, bootstrap 95% CI excluding zero); no recommendation flipped -- a sub-threshold regime invisible to standard QA but compounding across the thousands of decisions a deployed agent makes. CBL is orthogonal to known agent-failure axes (adversarial injection, cognitive degradation, multi-agent fault propagation, privacy leakage). We contribute an operational definition, a reusable protocol, a falsifiable prediction set, and a system-class characterization, establishing cross-module interference measurement as a requirement for prompt-composed agent evaluation.

### [202] [Accelerating Returns and the Qualitative Engine for Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26359)
*Guojun Liao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文批判性地分析了Kurzweil加速回报假说，指出其虽能解释执行性能力（如算力）的指数增长，但无法解决科学发现的核心问题——即对现有框架结构性不足的定性推理与概念创新。通过ARC-AGI-3基准测试中人类与AI的悬殊表现，论证了当前AI在灵活推理上的巨大鸿沟，并引入QES作为弥补该缺失能力的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kurzweil的加速回报假说是技术讨论中最具影响力的叙事之一，但其对科学发现核心问题的解释力尚未被充分审视。本文旨在通过数学诠释和实证案例，揭示该假说的适用范围边界，指出其无法处理科学发现中依赖于框架性定性推理的瓶颈问题。

Method: 1) 对加速回报假说进行简约的数学形式化诠释；2) 区分"执行性/基础设施能力"与"定性推理能力"两类不同认知功能；3) 引用ARC-AGI-3基准测试结果（人类天花板 vs AI<1%）作为实证支撑；4) 引入QES框架作为应对该缺失能力的回应方案。

Result: 论证了加速回报主要适用于执行性和基础设施能力（如算力增长），但科学发现中的框架转换与概念创新并不遵循此规律。ARC-AGI-3的结果强化了这一区分：人类灵活推理能力仍远超前沿AI系统。

Conclusion: Kurzweil的加速理论无法解决科学发现的核心问题；QES的价值在于它关注的是加速理论无法涵盖的领域——科学发现过程中需要被保存、组织和可访问的人类智慧。未来AI的发展不仅是技术预测问题，更是何种人类理解值得保留与传承的价值选择问题。

Abstract: Ray Kurzweil described a thesis of accelerating returns, which is the most influential narratives in discussions of technological progress. Its central claim is that advances in multiple technological fields, especially compute, artificial intelligence, brain science, and biotechnology, interact in such a way that progress becomes self-amplifying and approximately exponential. This paper gives a simple mathematical interpretation of that claim and then argues that, even if such acceleration is real, it does not by itself resolve the central problem of scientific discovery. The reason is that accelerating returns apply most naturally to executional and infrastructural capability, whereas genuine discovery often depends on a different capacity: qualitative reasoning about when a current framework is structurally inadequate and what conceptual move is needed next. Recent ARC-AGI-3 results sharpen this distinction: humans solve the benchmark at ceiling, whereas frontier AI systems remain below 1%, indicating that the gap between current AI and human flexible reasoning is still very large. At the same time, Demis Hassabis has emphasized that humans must retain their sense of meaning and what they choose to focus their lives on, a reminder that the future of AI is not only a technical forecast but also a question of what forms of human understanding are worth preserving and transmitting. This paper positions the Qualitative Engine for Science (QES) [3] as a response to that missing capacity. In this view, the Kurzweil theory helps explain why quantitative capability may accelerate, while QES addresses the central problem in scientific discovery that acceleration alone does not solve. Its value does not depend on when AGI arrives, but on the fact that the processes of scientific discovery themselves constitute a form of human wisdom worth preserving, organizing, and making accessible.

### [203] [Narration-of-Thought: Inference-Time Scaffolding for Defeasible Ethical Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26366)
*Patrick Cooper,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出叙述性思维(NoT)框架，通过结构化思维链为五个部分（主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、承诺），显著减少道德困境中的利益相关者崩溃和不确定性抑制问题，无需额外训练或微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准思维链在处理道德困境时存在两种失败模式：利益相关者崩溃（最多只提及一方利益相关者）和不确定性抑制（在承诺行动前缺乏明确的未知或保留表达），需要一种结构化方法来改善道德推理的全面性和透明度。

Method: 提出NoT系统提示，将思维链结构化为五个部分：主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、承诺。在100个DailyDilemmas场景上，使用来自三个供应商的四种生成器进行评估。通过匹配预算的冗长CoT控制实验排除token消耗因素，进行消融实验验证各部分贡献，并扩展为五轮多利益相关者辩论协议。

Result: NoT将利益相关者崩溃从最高31%降至低于1%，不确定性抑制从最高72%降至1-24%。在三种生成器上，利益相关者数量的Cliff's delta优势为+0.79至+0.90，不确定性评分为+0.65至+0.93。多利益相关者辩论协议将6%的僵局转化为95%的完全共识。

Conclusion: NoT框架能有效改善道德推理的全面性和透明性，提供可审计的推理轨迹，适用于可靠的智能体部署场景。

Abstract: Standard chain-of-thought on moral dilemmas exhibits two failure modes: stakeholder collapse (the trace names at most one party with a stake in the outcome) and uncertainty suppression (no explicit unknowns or hedges before committing to an action). We introduce narration-of-thought (NoT), a system prompt that structures chain-of-thought into five sections: protagonist, stakeholders, two-step consequences, uncertainty, then commitment. NoT adds no training, parameters, or fine-tuning. On 100 DailyDilemmas scenarios across four generators from three vendors, NoT cuts stakeholder collapse from up to 31% to under 1% and uncertainty suppression from up to 72% to 1-24% on every model. A matched-budget verbose-CoT control rules out token spend as the active ingredient; NoT retains Cliff's delta advantages of +0.79 to +0.90 on stakeholder count and +0.65 to +0.93 on uncertainty score for three of four generators, and a section ablation attributes each shift to its specific sub-instruction. Textual-gradient descent initialised at NoT improves the scaffold further; a cross-family training judge (different vendor from the generator) dominates an in-family one on every measured axis. Extended to a five-round multi-stakeholder debate protocol, the scaffold converts a 6% standoff into 95% full consensus on a calibration set and 100% combined convergence on a DailyDilemmas replication. The resulting traces externalise the stakeholders, consequences, and uncertainty grounding each commitment, providing an auditable substrate for dependable agentic deployment.

### [204] [Geometry-Aware MCTS for Extremal Problems in Combinatorial Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26399)
*Luoning Zhang,Xu Zhuang,Tianhao Wang,Nathan Kaplan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何感知的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）框架，用于解决组合几何中的极值问题（如No-Three-in-Line问题）。该方法通过增量更新可行动作空间严格施加几何约束，将共线点约束检查复杂度从O(n³)降至O(n²)，并利用几何对称性进行规范剪枝和对称批量转移提升搜索效率。在六个问题中的五个上取得了新的最佳已知计算结果，在Max-N3IL问题上对82≤n≤119的网格找到了约1.8n大小的配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合几何中的极值问题（如n×n网格上满足严格全局几何约束的点配置问题）面临三重挑战：经典精确求解器存在组合爆炸问题；标准强化学习和Transformer模型面临稀疏奖励的"有效性悬崖"以及二次令牌消耗限制。现有方法难以有效解决此类问题，亟需新的计算框架。

Method: 提出Geometry-Aware MCTS框架，核心包括：(1) 通过增量更新可行动作空间严格施加几何约束，将共线点约束检查复杂度从O(n³)降至O(n²)；(2) 利用几何对称性进行两种优化：节点扩展时的规范剪枝以降低分支因子，以及对称批量转移以加速有前景配置的发现。

Result: 在六个问题中的五个上取得了新的最佳已知计算结果。Max-N3IL问题中，对82≤n≤119的网格找到了约1.8n大小的配置；Smallest Complete Set问题中，找到了约0.95n大小的配置，为测试网格提供了新的上界。

Conclusion: Geometry-Aware MCTS被证明是一个高度自适应的框架，能够有效发现组合几何中的新配置，为这类受严格几何约束的极值组合问题提供了一种新的有效计算范式。

Abstract: We study certain extremal problems in combinatorial geometry that ask about configurations of points in an $n \times n$ grid that satisfy strict, global geometric constraints. Classical exact solvers suffer from combinatorial explosion for these types of problems, and standard reinforcement learning and transformer-based models struggle with the sparse reward "validity cliff" and quadratic token-consumption limits. To overcome these bottlenecks, we propose a Geometry-Aware Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) framework. Our approach strictly enforces geometric constraints through incremental updates to the feasible action space. For constraints about collections of collinear points, like those that occur in the classic No-Three-in-Line problem (Max-N3IL), this mechanism reduces the constraint checking complexity from $O(n^3)$ to $O(n^2)$. To improve search efficiency, we exploit geometric symmetries in two ways: canonical pruning during node expansion to reduce the branching factor, and symmetric batch transitions to accelerate the discovery of promising configurations. We perform extensive experiments and establish new best-known computational results on five out of six of the problems that we considered. Notably, for Max-N3IL we find configurations of size roughly $1.8 n$ for grids of size $82 \le n \le 119$. For the Smallest Complete Set problem, we find configurations of size roughly $0.95 n$, providing new upper bounds within the tested grids. This work establishes Geometry-Aware MCTS as a highly adaptable framework for discovering novel configurations in combinatorial geometry.

### [205] [When Agents Meet Electric Bus Fleet Operations: Pricing Behavior, Trade-offs, and Policy Implications in an Aggregator Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26400)
*Jônatas Augusto Manzolli,Ali Eslami,Luis Miranda-Moreno,Jiangbo Yu*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Agent的聚合框架，将优化驱动的电动公交车调度模型与监督型智能体（用于扰动检测、电价自适应和调度评估）相结合，实现了电动公交车队在V2G环境下的自适应协调调度。通过在真实场站的日前与实时运行实验，验证了该框架在多种扰动下保持调度可行性、选择性触发重优化并提升充放电灵活性的能力，同时也揭示了以利润为导向的协调模式可能从公交运营商处抽取价值，需要在公共车队部署中建立透明的定价与价值共享机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电动公交车队的运行需要持续协调服务可靠性、电池荷电状态、充电桩可用性、电价、路线能量不确定性和V2G机会等多个异构因素，传统优化方法难以灵活应对动态变化的运行条件，因此需要一种能够自适应协调上述复杂决策环境的框架。

Method: 提出Agentic Aggregator框架，底层为基于优化的电动公交车调度模型（保障路线、充电桩、电池和V2G交换的物理可行性），上层为监督型智能体层（扰动检测智能体、电价自适应智能体、调度评估智能体），实时监测运行条件变化并按需触发重优化，同时定义聚合商与公交运营商之间的灵活性价值分配机制。

Result: Agentic聚合能够维持可行调度、选择性激活重优化并改善充电与V2G灵活性的利用效率；但在利润导向的协调模式下，Agent能力可能从公交运营商处抽取价值，揭示了适应性能力与价值分配之间的关键权衡。

Conclusion: Agentic聚合器在管理电动公交车V2G运行方面具有实用价值，但在公共车队场景中部署时需要透明的协调模式、可审计的电价设定机制以及明确的价值共享规则。

Abstract: Agentic systems are changing how complex operational tasks are coordinated, introducing a new paradigm for connecting heterogeneous data sources and automating processes. Electric bus fleets provide a relevant test case. Their operation requires continuous coordination between service reliability, battery state-of-charge, charger availability, electricity prices, route-energy uncertainty, and vehicle-to-grid (V2G) opportunities. This paper proposes an agentic aggregator framework that streamlines this decision environment by coupling an optimization-based electric bus scheduling model with supervisory agents for disturbance detection, tariff adaptation, and schedule evaluation. The optimization core enforces physical feasibility across routes, chargers, batteries, and V2G exchanges, while the agentic layer interprets changing operating conditions, triggers real-time re-optimization when needed, and defines how flexibility value is allocated between the aggregator and the public transport operator (PTO). A realistic depot case study evaluates day-ahead and real-time operations under profit-based and operation-based coordination modes, considering service delays, route-energy deviations, electricity price shocks, and combined disturbances. The results show that agentic aggregation can support adaptive fleet-grid coordination by maintaining feasible schedules, activating re-optimization selectively, and improving the use of charging and V2G flexibility. However, they also reveal a critical trade-off: the same agentic capability that reduces operational complexity can extract value from the PTO when configured around profit-oriented pricing. These findings suggest that agentic aggregators can become useful for managing electric bus V2G operations, but their deployment in public-fleet contexts requires transparent coordination modes, auditable tariff-setting, and explicit value-sharing rules.

### [206] [Unbiased Canonical Set-Valued Oracles Via Lattice Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26418)
*Jobst Heitzig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对非智能体“预言机”AI在估计未来事件概率时面临的自指问题，提出了一种基于可信集（credal set）的自指替代方案。该方案利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，在封闭可信集的完备格上取最小不动点，得到既无偏又自洽的规范答案。作者证明了存在性、自洽性和非空性，并展示了该构造在非表演性问题下退化为经典点估计，在二元事件下规范答案为区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非智能体预言机在回答概率估计问题时面临自指困境：其答案一旦被获知并采取行动，就会改变它原本被要求报告的概率。一个现有方案（Scientist AI方案）只回答反事实问题，但这类答案在被告知后立即变得无关紧要。因此，需要探索一种能够处理自指问题的替代方案。

Method: 本文不报告单一概率，而是报告一个可信集（credal set），要求该集合同时满足无偏性和与答案被学习后的后果自洽。利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，在封闭可信集的完备格上定义保序算子，取其最小不动点作为规范答案；另有一种变体取包含所有自洽点估计的最小不动点。该构造从二元事件自然推广到任意随机变量。

Result: 证明了规范答案的存在性、自洽性和非空性；展示了该构造在非表演性问题（non-performative questions）下退化为经典点估计；在二元事件下，在自然的包络分解假设下，规范答案为区间。该构造从二元事件B推广到任意随机变量X，将条件概率P(B|A,C)替换为条件律L(X|A,C)。

Conclusion: 本文提供了处理概率预言机自指问题的格论框架，得到了规范的、非平凡的自洽可信集。但仍有开放问题，包括区间刻画是否能从二元事件推广到一般随机变量。

Abstract: A non-agentic "oracle" AI that estimates probabilities of future events faces a self-reference problem: once its answer is learned and acted upon, it can change the very probability it was asked to report. One response, advocated for the Scientist AI programme, is to ask only counterfactual questions, evaluated as if the answer had no influence. We observe that such answers tend to become irrelevant the moment they are learned, precisely because their premise is then false. We therefore explore a self-referential alternative in which the oracle reports not a single probability but a credal set that is simultaneously unbiased and self-consistent with the consequences of being learned. The naive self-consistency requirement is satisfied by too many sets (including the useless answer $[0,1]$), so the problem is to single out a canonical, nontrivial member. We do so with the Knaster--Tarski fixed-point theorem on the complete lattice of closed credal sets, taking the least fixed point of a suitably defined isotone operator; a variant instead reports the least fixed point that contains every self-consistent point estimate. We prove existence, self-consistency, and nonemptiness, show that the construction collapses to the classical point answer for non-performative questions, and that for a binary event the canonical answer is, under a natural hull-factoring assumption, an interval. The development is purely lattice-theoretic and extends unchanged from a binary event $B$ to an arbitrary random variable $X$, with $P(B\mid A,C)$ replaced by the conditional law $\mathcal{L}(X\mid A,C)$. We close with open questions, including whether the interval characterization itself survives that generalization.

</details>


### [207] [Estimating Uncertainty in Classifier Performance with Applications to Large Language Models and Nested Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26422)
*Kylie Anglin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了社会科学校验集场景下分类性能指标置信区间方法的准确性，发现Wald区间和基本百分位Bootstrap在样本量小、构念稀疏时覆盖不足，而Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson及一种新颖的正则化伪计数Bootstrap（尤其适用于F1）表现更优；当文本嵌套于个体时，需同时调整有效N和自由度，层次Bootstrap优于聚类Bootstrap但少量文本时偏保守。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究人员在报告文本分类性能指标（召回率、精确率等）时，通常仅给出点估计而不报告不确定性的置信区间；即便报告，所用方法在小标注集或高性能条件下不适当。本文旨在系统评估并推荐适合社会科学文本分类场景的置信区间方法。

Method: 通过模拟实验，在社会科学典型条件（中小样本量、稀疏构念、文本嵌套于个体）下，比较了Wald区间、基本百分位Bootstrap、Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson及一种新颖的正则化伪计数Bootstrap等多种置信区间方法的准确性。

Result: Wald区间和基本百分位Bootstrap覆盖最不准确，有时远低于名义95%水平；Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson和正则化伪计数Bootstrap准确性更高；文本嵌套时需同时调整有效N和自由度；层次Bootstrap在文本量适中时优于聚类Bootstrap，但文本量极少时偏保守。

Conclusion: 建议社会科学文本分类研究应使用更准确的置信区间方法（如Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson或正则化伪计数Bootstrap），提高机器学习应用透明度，并在设计阶段关注校验样本量。

Abstract: Researchers increasingly use text classification--supervised models or large language models--to measure constructs from natural language, providing metrics such as recall and precision as evidence of their validity. Yet, though these metrics are point estimates subject to sampling variation, measures of uncertainty are inconsistently reported alongside them. Further, when they are reported, they are often estimated with methods that are not appropriate when relevant labelled datasets are small or performance is high. To increase and improve confidence interval reporting in the field, this paper evaluates confidence interval methods for performance metrics under conditions typical of social science text classification: small to moderate sample sizes, infrequent constructs, and texts nested within individuals. Across simulations, default methods such as the Wald interval and the basic percentile bootstrap are the least accurate, with coverage sometimes far below the nominal 95% level. Accuracy is improved with the use of Agresti-Coull, Wilson, Clopper-Pearson, and a novel pseudo-count regularized bootstrap (which is particularly relevant to the calculation of F1). When texts are nested within individuals, we demonstrate that adjustment for both effective N and the appropriate degrees of freedom is necessary for producing accurate analytic intervals. Among bootstrap intervals, the hierarchical bootstrap is more accurate than the cluster bootstrap when individuals produce a moderate number of texts but overly conservative when individuals produce only a few. By providing guidance to the field on appropriate interval estimation, we aim to improve the transparency of machine learning applications, and to encourage greater attention to the validation sample size at the design stage.

</details>


### [208] [Data-driven Machine Learning Cannot Reach Symbolic-level Logical Reasoning -- The Limit of the Scaling Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26454)
*Tiansi Dong,Mateja Jamnik,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文证明了监督深度学习由于训练数据无法区分所有24种有效三段论推理类型，以及端到端映射在模式识别与逻辑推理组件间引入矛盾训练目标这两个方法论局限，无法达到符号级三段论推理的严谨性。实验表明Euler Net无法完成严格三段论推理，ChatGPT（GPT-5）虽可达100%准确率但解释有误，因此监督机器学习系统无法达到符号逻辑推理的严谨水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究数据驱动的机器学习系统能否通过增加训练数据和训练时间达到符号级三段论推理水平，即逻辑推理的规模定律极限所在。

Method: 理论分析指出监督深度学习的两个方法论局限，并通过Euler Net和ChatGPT（GPT-5-nano和GPT-5）在四种表面形式（单词、双词、简单符号、长随机符号）下的三段论可满足性判断实验进行验证。

Result: Euler Net无法实现严格三段论推理；ChatGPT GPT-5虽可达100%准确率，但推理解释存在错误；表面形式影响推理性能。

Conclusion: 由于监督学习在达到100%准确率后即停止训练，无法纠正解释错误，因此监督机器学习系统无法达到符号逻辑推理的严谨性水平。

Abstract: Sphere neural networks have achieved symbolic level syllogistic reasoning without training data, raising the question of where the limit of the scaling law for logical reasoning lies, i.e., whether data-driven machine learning systems can achieve the same level by increasing training data and training time. We show two methodological limitations that prevent supervised deep learning from reaching the symbolic-level syllogistic reasoning: (1) training data can not distinguish all 24 types of valid syllogistic reasoning; (2) end-to-end mapping from premises to conclusion introduces contradictory training targets between neural components for pattern recognition and logical reasoning. Beside theoretical analysis, we experimentally illustrate that Euler Net cannot achieve rigorous syllogistic reasoning. We further challenge the most recent ChatGPTs (GPT-5-nano and GPT-5) to determine the satisfiability of syllogistic statements in four surface forms (patterns): words, double words, simple symbols, and long random symbols, showing that surface forms affect the reasoning performance and that ChatGPT GPT-5 may reach 100% accuracy but still provide incorrect explanations. As empirical training processes are stopped after achieving 100% accuracy, we conclude that supervised machine learning systems will not attain the rigour of symbolic logical reasoning.

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) over knowledge graphs has emerged as a promising approach for grounding large language models, yet existing benchmarks largely overlook the challenges of retrieval in multimodal knowledge graph RAG (MKG-RAG). To address this gap, we introduce MKG-RAG-Bench, a cross-domain benchmark explicitly designed to evaluate retrieval in MKG-RAG. MKG-RAG-Bench is constructed from two multimodal knowledge graphs spanning general and medical domains, and includes carefully aligned question-answering datasets that support controlled evaluation of both retrieval and downstream generation. The benchmark is built using an LLM-based curation pipeline that filters low-utility knowledge, generates structurally grounded queries with exact supervision, and systematically covers diverse modality configurations. Through extensive experiments across representative retriever families and modality settings, we show that effective multimodal retrieval remains challenging yet crucial for end-to-end MKG-RAG performance, and that retrieval quality strongly determines generation outcomes. By isolating retrieval as a first-class evaluation target, MKG-RAG-Bench provides a principled foundation for diagnosing current limitations and advancing multimodal knowledge graph RAG systems.

Psychology, and computational cognitive science in particular, is well-positioned to benefit from AI experimentation because theories are often represented as code and crowdsourcing platforms enable programmatic human data collection at scale. Here, we apply automated discovery techniques to the project of generating theories in computational cognitive science, with an agent-based system collecting human data independently through crowdsourced survey experiments. As a testbed, we use a classic case study from cognitive psychology: judging which sequences of coin flips seem subjectively more random. Our system, auto-psych, uses nested agent-based discovery loops to generate explanatory theories of human behavior. The inner loop conjectures, fits, and critiques probabilistic cognitive models; the outer loop designs experiments to test these models, launches them online, and analyzes the data. This system can quickly and reliably recover ground-truth theories from synthetic data via systematic experimentation, but the nested structure is critical to model performance. Further, in three independent sequences of human experiments, the system finds theories that fit the data better than theories generated from the scientific literature. This work thus demonstrates the feasibility of automated data collection and theory discovery in computational cognitive science.

### [212] [Humans Disengage, Reasoning Models Persist: Separating Difficulty Registration from Deliberation Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26502)
*Han-yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型推理模型（LRM）在难题上花费更多token（跨项目注册与人类一致），但在同一项目内部，LRM答错时反而比答对时花费更多token，而人类则相反（分配模式相反）。这种分离在固定项目效应下显著，揭示了两种不同的停止策略：人类是“投入vs放弃”，LRM是“不确定性驱动长度”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示LRM与人类在问题解决过程中的认知资源分配模式的根本差异，指出表面相似（跨项目难度-时间正相关）下隐藏的相反分配模式（同一项目内正确/错误时的token消耗方向相反）。

Method: 在人类-LRM配对语料库上，分离两个分析层次：跨项目的难度-时间注册（registration）和固定项目内的资源分配（allocation）。对比人类与5种thinking LRM在H-ARC等数据集上的表现，使用Cohen's d量化效应量，并加入非thinking基线对照。

Result: 所有LRM在跨项目层面复现了人类的正相关注册模式，但在固定项目内，LRM的错误尝试比正确尝试消耗更多token（Cohen's d=1.47-3.13），而人类则相反。该分离在固定效应检验下显著，跨数据集可复现，且在非thinking模型中不存在。

Conclusion: 人类和LRM采用了基于相同难度信号但相反控制策略的两种停止策略：人类在预期能解决时投入、否则放弃（engagement vs abandonment）；LRM则在不确定时延长推理链，而正是这种不确定导致失败。资源理性元推理框架下，trace长度捕捉到难度信号但掩盖了控制策略的差异。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) take longer on harder problems, just as humans do. This surface similarity hides an opposite pattern within items. When an LRM gets a problem wrong, it spends more tokens than when it gets the same problem right; humans do the reverse, spending less time on the trials they get wrong. We separate two levels of deliberation: how response time tracks difficulty across items (registration), and, with item identity held fixed, whether an agent spends more on its own failures or successes (allocation). On a public matched human-LRM corpus, humans and all five thinking LRMs reproduce the known cross-item alignment (registration) but diverge within items (allocation): every LRM shows a large wrong-vs-right effect (Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13 on H-ARC) while humans show the opposite sign. The comparison stays inside each agent's own scale; we never put seconds and tokens on one axis. The dissociation holds under item fixed effects, replicates across datasets, and is absent in a non-thinking baseline. We read the human pattern as engagement versus abandonment: people stay on items they expect to solve and give up on the rest. We read the LRM pattern as length driven by uncertainty: chains grow when the model is unsure, which is exactly when it tends to fail. Both policies produce the same cross-item correlation with difficulty, so they look aligned on the measure prior work has used; the divergence shows up only once item identity is fixed. Under resource-rational metareasoning, the split is between two stopping policies that share a difficulty signal but implement opposite control; trace length captures the signal and misses the control.

</details>

Existing EEG toolkits provide excellent offline analysis, but assembling a real-time, quality-gated cognitive-load pipeline often requires manually bridging acquisition, custom QC, Alpha feature extraction, and a web API; this tutorial closes that offline-to-online gap. The tutorial uses a quality-gated workflow: downstream Alpha and workload metrics are computed only after preprocessing and QC gating rather than directly from raw EEG. In the included mini-dataset validation, the agent processed 18 recordings, generated 10 within-subject comparisons, observed task-related posterior Alpha suppression in 7 of 10 contrasts, estimated initial evidence of within-subject repeatability, and benchmarked local online API latency. Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can make scientific software easier to use. These distinctions are especially important for low-channel electroencephalography (EEG), where sparse spatial coverage and variable signal quality make plausible but unsupported interpretations easy to produce. We present NeuraDock Agent, an open-source architecture that separates a deterministic local EEG engine from a hardware-aware language layer. The numerical engine parses recordings, performs quality control, executes reviewed spectral workflows, and writes machine-readable artifacts. The LLM receives only a compact, allowlisted summary and a versioned context pack. The context describes the seven-channel hardware, reviewed workflows, result fields, implementation boundaries, scientific limits, and reference cases. Raw EEG and dense per-sample arrays remain local

First, 12 recordings produced identical structured results over ten numerical repetitions, and a complete Rest/Task run produced identical result, report, and figure hashes over three repetitions. Second, request-capture and failure-injection experiments confirmed the tested data boundary and preservation of local artifacts under HTTP, malformed-output, and connection failures. Third, a boundary-awareness benchmark tested 36 ordinary and adversarial questions under four context ablations and two LLMs, yielding 288 outputs.These results support hardware- and implementation-aware grounding as a practical mechanism for calibrating what an EEG agent accepts, qualifies, or refuses; they do not establish clinical validity or a validated absolute cognitive-load index.

### [215] [Radical AI Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26523)
*Daniel A. Herrmann,Benjamin A. Levinstein*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个将AI系统解释为智能体的框架，结合哲学传统中的激进诠释学与机械可解释性工具，探讨如何从系统的计算事实中求解其信念、欲望和意义。核心观点是这些属性不能孤立地归因，而必须整体性地联合约束，这对AI安全与欺骗检测具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统的部署日益广泛，如何信任这些系统——无论是理解其目标还是检测其欺骗行为——成为一个关键安全问题。当前的可解释性研究虽然能够从模型内部读取信念和欲望，但缺乏一套成熟的标准来判断这些归因是否成功，本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 借鉴激进诠释学的哲学传统，结合机械可解释性的技术工具，提出了表征主义（representationalist）和诠释主义（interpretationist）两种路径的评价标准，并将其与当前可解释性方法可执行的测试相连接。强调信念、欲望和命题结构三者之间的整体性约束关系。

Result: 得出核心结论：AI系统的态度归因不能以孤立的方式进行，信念、欲望和命题结构是联合约束的；系统的态度约束其命题结构，命题结构又反过来约束可归因的态度；机械可解释性可以帮助同时测量这两个方面，从而获得更可靠的归因。

Conclusion: 本文为AI系统的信念、欲望和意义归因提供了理论框架和评价标准，强调了整体性约束的重要性，并为可解释性研究提供了新的方法论指导。这一框架对于提升AI系统部署的安全性、可靠性和可信任度具有重要价值。

Abstract: We develop a framework for interpreting AI systems as agents, drawing on the philosophical tradition of radical interpretation and the tools of mechanistic interpretability. The core question is: given the computational facts about a system, how do we solve for its beliefs, desires, and meanings? This matters increasingly for safety. We want to be able to trust the systems we deploy, whether by understanding their goals or, more modestly, by reliably detecting deception. Interpretability researchers are building tools to read beliefs and desires off a model's internals, but there is no settled account of when such a tool has succeeded. This book supplies one. We propose criteria on both representationalist and interpretationist approaches, and tie each to tests current interpretability methods can carry out. A central lesson is that these attributions cannot be made piecemeal. Beliefs, desires, and the propositional structure they presuppose are jointly constrained, and a method that fixes one while measuring the others inherits whatever distortions that introduces. This holism becomes pressing for AI systems, which may not share the interpreter's concepts. However, it also provides leverage: a system's attitudes constrain its propositional structure, that structure constrains which attitudes can be attributed, and mechanistic interpretability can help us measure both.

</details>


### [216] [PMDformer: Patch-Mean Decoupling Information Transformer for Long-term Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26549)
*Ao Hu,Liangjian Wen,Jiang Duan,Yong Dai,He Yan,Dongkai Wang,Jun Wang,Yukun Zhang,Ruoxi Jiang,Zenglin Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PMDformer模型，通过补丁均值解耦（PMD）、趋势恢复注意力（TRA）和邻近变量注意力（PVA）三个模块，解决了长序列时间序列预测中跨补丁和跨变量的形状相似性建模问题，在多个基准数据集上取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Transformer的LTSF模型采用补丁策略捕获长程依赖，但由于尺度差异，难以准确建模跨补丁和跨变量的形状相似性。

Method: 1) PMD：对每个补丁减去均值，分离趋势和残差形状信息，使注意力机制捕获真实形状相似性；2) TRA：在计算注意力输出时重新整合PMD解耦的趋势；3) PVA：将跨变量注意力聚焦于最相关的近期时间段，避免对过时相关性的过拟合。

Result: 在多个LTSF基准数据集上，PMDformer在稳定性和准确性上均优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: PMDformer通过补丁均值解耦与针对性注意力机制，有效提升了长序列时间序列预测中形状相似性的建模能力，为LTSF任务提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting (LTSF) plays a crucial role in fields such as energy management, finance, and traffic prediction. Transformer-based models have adopted patch-based strategies to capture long-range dependencies, but accurately modeling shape similarities across patches and variables remains challenging due to scale differences. To address this, we introduce patch-mean decoupling (PMD), which separates the trend and residual shape information by subtracting the mean of each patch, preserving the original structure and ensuring that the attention mechanism captures true shape similarities. Futhermore, to more effectively model long-range dependencies and capture cross-variable relationships, we propose Trend Restoration Attention (TRA) and Proximal Variable Attention (PVA). The former module reintegrates the decoupled trend from PMD while calculating attention output. And the latter focuses cross-variable attention on the most relevant, recent time segments to avoid overfitting on outdated correlations. Combining these components, we propose PMDformer, a model designed to effectively capture shape similarity in long-term forecasting scenarios. Extensive experiments indicate that PMDformer outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods in stability and accuracy across multiple LTSF benchmarks. The code is available at https://github.com/aohu1105/PMDformer.

</details>

Abstract: Hepatitis C is a liver infection caused by a virus, which results in mild to severe inflammation of the liver. Over many years, hepatitis C gradually damages the liver, often leading to permanent scarring, known as cirrhosis. Patients sometimes have moderate or no symptoms of liver illness for decades before developing cirrhosis. Cirrhosis typically worsens to the point of liver failure. Patients with cirrhosis may also experience brain and nerve system damage, as well as gastrointestinal hemorrhage. Treatment for cirrhosis focuses on preventing further progression of the disease. Detecting cirrhosis earlier is therefore crucial for avoiding complications. Machine learning (ML) has been shown to be effective at providing precise and accurate information for use in diagnosing several diseases. Despite this, no studies have so far used ML to detect cirrhosis in patients with hepatitis C. This study obtained a dataset consisting of 28 attributes of 2038 Egyptian patients from the ML Repository of the University of California at Irvine. Four ML algorithms were trained on the dataset to diagnose cirrhosis in hepatitis C patients: a Random Forest, a Gradient Boosting Machine, an Extreme Gradient Boosting, and an Extra Trees model. The Extra Trees model outperformed the other models achieving an accuracy of 96.92%, a recall of 94.00%, a precision of 99.81%, and an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve of 96% using only 16 of the 28 features.

### [218] [EvoOptiGraph: Weakness-Driven Coevolution via Graph-Based Structural Generation for Optimization Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26578)
*Qingcan Kang,Mingyang Liu,Xiaojin Fu,Shixiong Kai,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出EvoOptiGraph框架，通过数据与模型的协同进化（基于模型弱点生成结构多样的MILP实例），结合SFT和RLVR两阶段训练，在优化建模任务上显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的自动化优化建模面临两个关键挑战：训练语料缺乏结构多样性，以及数据生成管线是静态的、与模型学习脱节。

Method: 将MILP表示为属性二分图，应用保持有效性的进化算子生成结构多样实例；通过确定性编译和验证反向翻译转换为求解器代码和自然语言；两阶段训练：先监督微调（SFT），再基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），由图的弱点信号引导针对模型失败生成新实例，形成闭环持续更新训练分布。

Result: 在六个公开数据集上，EvoOptiGraph在准确性、可执行性和泛化性上显著优于更大的通用模型、智能体方法和专门基线。

Conclusion: 目标导向的数据-模型协同进化是提升LLM在优化建模任务上表现的有效策略。

Abstract: Automating optimization modeling from natural language with large language models (LLMs) faces two key challenges. First, training corpora lack structural diversity. Second, data generation pipelines remain static and decoupled from model learning. To address these challenges, we propose EvoOptiGraph, a novel framework where data and model co-evolve, driven by model weaknesses. EvoOptiGraph represents each mixed-integer linear program (MILP) as an attributed bipartite graph and applies validity-preserving evolutionary operators to generate structurally diverse instances. The evolved graphs are converted into solver code and natural language via deterministic compilation and verified back-translation. Training proceeds in two stages: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on an initial dataset, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where graph-derived weakness signals guide the generation of new instances targeting the model's failures. This forms a closed loop that continuously updates the training distribution. Empirical results on six public datasets show that EvoOptiGraph significantly outperforms larger generalist models, agentic methods, and specialized baselines in accuracy, executability, and generalization. These results demonstrate that targeted data-model coevolution is an effective strategy for improving LLMs on optimization modeling tasks.

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SkillDisCo框架，将任务成功轨迹中的共享过程结构蒸馏为可复用的参数化控制流子图（PFSM），并编译为可调用、可执行、可验证的过程技能，在ALFWorld和WebArena上提升了成功率并减少了agent交互轮次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SkillDisCo框架包含两个阶段：(1)蒸馏阶段，从成功轨迹中提取可复用的参数化有限状态机（PFSM）子图；(2)编译阶段，将蒸馏得到的子图编译为可调用、可执行且可验证的过程技能。

Abstract: Agents often repeatedly solve similar task instances from scratch, leading to unnecessary reasoning cost and long execution traces. Prior work has explored workflow reuse and executable skill induction, but it remains unclear which task scenarios admit procedural skills and how the shared procedural structure should be represented across successful traces. We study this problem in FSM-defined scenarios, where successful traces can be viewed as paths in an unknown transition graph, and formulate procedural skills as reusable parameterized control-flow subgraphs. Based on this view, we introduce SkillDisCo, a distillation-and-compilation framework that distills reusable PFSM subgraphs from successful traces and compiles them into callable, executable, and verifiable procedural skills. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebArena show that SkillDisCo improves success rates and reduces agent turns across benchmarks and model scales, demonstrating the benefits of representing shared experience as reusable execution structures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建384万多源SFT样本和20万可验证RL候选池，设计端到端数据处理堆栈（响应蒸馏、多维交叉验证过滤、细粒度难度分级、任务分类和多样性感知采样）。指令分支采用三阶段优化SFT方法NebulaExp-Ins-SFT，再经GRPO强化学习；推理分支采用中等难度GRPO RL；系统研究单教师和多教师OPD方法（MOPD）以解决RL对任务验证器的依赖。

Result: Instruct分支：SFT将平均基准得分从55.01提升至60.99，GRPO进一步升至61.85。Reasoning分支：中等难度GRPO RL将平均推理得分从73.88提升至75.17。MOPD仅用4K指令跟随样本，在IFEval上超越RL基线3.26分，平均增益+4.43；融合4个领域专家教师仅用10K样本，平均性能提升4.18。

Conclusion: 提供了一个完全可复现的8B规模LLM经验性后训练配方，并全面剖析了指令遵循、数学推理、代码生成和通用知识之间的能力权衡。

Abstract: Post-training alignment determines the reasoning and human preference following capabilities of large language models, yet most existing works withhold detailed data construction, filtering rules and training recipes, which hinders community reproducibility and lightweight model optimization. This work presents NebulaExp, a fully transparent, ablation-driven post-training pipeline built on Qwen3-8B-base, covering two orthogonal model branches: general instruct model and complex reasoning-specialized model. We curate a raw corpus of 3.84M multi-source SFT samples and a 200K verifiable RL candidate pool, and design an end-to-end data processing stack including response distillation, multi-dimensional cross-verification filtering, fine-grained difficulty grading, task classification and diversity-aware sampling. For the Instruct branch, our three-stage optimized supervised fine-tuning approach NebulaExp-Ins-SFT improves the average benchmark score from the 55.01 baseline of Qwen3-8B-nothink to 60.99. GRPO reinforcement learning then further elevates the average score to 61.85. For the Reasoning branch, medium-difficulty GRPO RL improves average reasoning score from 73.88 to 75.17. To address RL's dependency on task verifiers, we systematically investigate single-teacher and multi-teacher OPD (MOPD): utilizing merely 4K instruction-following samples and outperforms RL baseline by 3.26 points on IFEval with +4.43 average overall gain; MOPD fuses four domain-specialist teachers with merely 10K samples, lifting average performance by 4.18 over the base model. This report provides a fully reproducible empirical post-training recipe for 8B-scale LLMs, and comprehensively dissects the capability trade-offs among instruction adherence, mathematical reasoning, code generation and general knowledge.

</details>


### [225] [Do Safety Guardrails Need to Reason? LeanGuard: A Fast and Light Approach for Robust Moderation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26686)
*Dongbin Na*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出LeanGuard，一种轻量级无推理的安全护栏模型。通过控制变量实验证明，链式推理（CoT）并未提升内容审核的准确性。LeanGuard（395M参数）仅需单次前向传播，平均F1达82.90，在推理计算量减少约100倍的情况下，性能与基于更大解码器的推理护栏相当，且在标签噪声和严格假阳性率下表现更鲁棒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全护栏方法普遍采用链式推理（CoT）来提升决策质量，但这导致模型生成大量token后才做判定，变得沉重、缓慢，不适合资源受限的部署场景（如机器人端侧）。作者质疑：安全护栏是否真的需要推理？

Method: 在一个可控的相同基础对比框架下，训练轻量级双向编码器（标签-only）和推理护栏，然后移除推理部分，保持其他所有设置不变。由此得到的LeanGuard仅需对最多512个token的输入进行一次前向传播即可输出判定结果。

Result: LeanGuard（395M参数）在公开基准上平均F1达82.90±0.26，性能与基于更大解码器的推理护栏相当；推理计算量减少约100倍；在训练标签噪声下保持鲁棒，在严格假阳性率下召回率远高于推理护栏。

Conclusion: 当前护栏基准可能难度不够，不足以让推理发挥优势；CoT对于内容审核的必要性尚未被证明。更重的推理护栏并非更鲁棒的选择。

Abstract: In order to screen a prompt or a response, the recent guardrail methods generate a chain-of-thought (CoT) before they issue a verdict. This design follows a common belief that step-by-step reasoning improves a decision. However, CoT also makes the guard heavy and slow, because the model must generate many tokens before it decides. This may not match how guardrails are actually deployed. A guardrail sometimes should not be heavy and slow, and it often runs on-device, for example on an embodied robot. In this paper, we pose a question whether a safety guardrail really needs to reason. To answer this question, we train a lightweight bidirectional encoder and a reasoning guard on the same corpus, and we then remove only the reasoning while we keep everything else fixed. With this controlled same-base comparison, we show that the chain does not improve moderation accuracy. We name the resulting guard LeanGuard. A 395M label-only encoder reaches an average F1 of 82.90 $\pm$ 0.26 over public benchmarks. It matches a reasoning guard that is built on a much larger decoder, while it uses only a single forward pass over an input of at most 512 tokens. This is about a ~100x reduction in inference compute. We further show that this label-only encoder stays robust under training-label noise and retains far more recall at a strict false-positive rate than the reasoning guard, so a heavier reasoning guard is not the more robust choice either. Our finding suggests that the current guardrail benchmarks may not be hard enough to reward reasoning, and that the necessity of CoT for moderation is still not proven. We release all source codes and models including LeanGuard at https://github.com/ndb796/LeanGuard.

</details>
